The  Farmer’s  Dog 
  
INTRODUCTION  /  FOUNDERS  
STORY
 
 
Hi,
 
I'm
 
Brett.
 
 
And
 
I'm
 
Jonathan.
 
 
This
 
is
 
Darla
 
and
 
this
 
is
 
Buddy.

the

of

Farmer's
 
Dog.
 
 
We've

an

new

to

THE  ORIGIN  STORY  
 
It
 
all
 
started
 
with
 
my
 
ﬁrst
 
dog,
 
Jada.
 
 
I

Jada
 
in

twenties.

ﬁrst

She

but

constantly

No  things  seemed  to  help  her  until  a  vet  recommended  that  I  started  home  
cooking
 
for
 
her.
 
 
All
 
of
 
her
 
issues
 
went
 
away.
 
Her

changed.
 
DISCOVERY  OF  THE  PROBLEM  WITH  PET  FOOD  
 
We
 
started
 
going
 
down
 
this
 
journey
 
of
 
looking
 
into
 
what
 
is
 
dog
 
food?
 
How
 
is

Kibble  can  be  made  with  ingredients  that  would  be  illegal  to  sell  to  a  human  
for
 
consumption,
 
then
 
turned
 
into
 
a

using
 
extreme
 
heat,
 
extruded
 
into
 
the
 
brown
 
balls
 
we
 
all
 
know…
 
and
 
then
 
sprayed
 
with
 
nutrients
 
and

so

dogs
 
will
 
actually

We  were  told  kibble  was  the  best  thing  you  could  feed  your  dog  —  premium

Turns
 
out

We

That's

It

90

for

NASA

AC

The

that's

down
 
any
 
room

SI  Joint  Pain  Relief   
  
HOOK  –  CALLING  OUT  THE  SPECIFIC  PAIN  
 
Si,
 
joint
 
pain,
 
pain
 
in
 
these
 
bony
 
spots
 
in
 
your
 
lower
 
back,
 
right
 
next
 
to
 
your
 
tailbone.
 
 
It's
 
actually
 
coming
 
from
 
the
 
front
 
of
 
your

ROOT  CAUSE  EXPLANATION  
 
There's
 
this
 
muscle
 
here
 
called
 
your
 
iliacs
 
muscle.
 
 
This
 
big
 
one
 
here,
 
when
 
it's
 
tight,
 
it
 
pulls
 
your

forward,
 
rotates
 
it
 
forward,
 
and
 
actually
 
puts
 
strain
 
on
 
when
 
your

  But  over  the  years,  especially  after  the  age  of  40,  your  muscles  can  stop  responding

=== PAGE 107 ===

In  a  recent  study  from  the  University  of  North  Dakota.    Scientists  took  130  people  with  sarcopenia,  a  k,  a  severe  muscle  loss.  The  researcher

crazy

  And  while  leucine  is  already  one  of  the  most  powerful  ways  of  growing  muscle.    This  next  amino  acid  gives  even  more  impressive  results. [Instructions  on  how  to  use  information]   To  get  them  out,  slice  up  to  5  lemons,  and  boil  them  in  a  gallon  and  a  half  of  water. of
 
critical
 
nutrients.
 
  But  when  you  cook  potatoes  in  a  pressure  cooker,  most  lectins  are  deactivated.    And  it’s  especially  important  to  peel  potatoes,  because  thats  where  the  highest  concentration  of  
lectins
 
are.
 
  See,  most  people  don’t  realize  that  if  any  lectin-heavy  food  isn’t  properly  prepared,  it  can  
seriously
 
damage
 
gut
 
health.
